(5) `valenx-surface`'s `remove_knot` apply loop had an off-by-one (`temp[i-first]` vs `temp[i-first+1]`) and a wrong CP-removal index — knot insertion then removal did not round-trip. (6) `valenx-gcad3d`'s three-point-arc circumcentre formula had both cross-product terms sign-flipped (centre reflected through `p1`); and 5 of its stroke-font glyphs (`G U 2 6 8 9`) were drawn with arcs bulging outside the unit box. (7) `valenx-cam` / `valenx-camotics-sim` surface-nets placed grid samples at voxel *corners* not *centres*, so the smoothed surface bulged outside the stock. (8) `valenx-decimate-pro`'s cot-Laplacian mean curvature reported spurious non-zero values at boundary vertices (open one-ring) — added boundary detection. (9) `valenx-defeaturing`'s sliver detector used `min_edge / max_edge`, which misses a near-zero-area "cap" triangle with well-proportioned edges — switched to the area-based min-altitude / longest-edge thinness. The 10 wrong tests included off-screen pick/box-select coordinates that missed their intended target, a distance-mate-drag scenario that contradicted the function's documented "drag wins" contract, a `PanelId`-is-`&str` doc-test, a Hermite-overshoot test with a wrong premise, and the surface-nets-vs-faceted triangle-count misconception (a binary-grid dual scheme emits one quad per sign-changing edge — *equal* triangle count to faceted, the win is vertex *sharing*). All 24 crates now fully green (`valenx-cam` keeps 1 pre-existing unrelated `rest_machining` `#[ignore]`). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). ~600 LOC. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`. The remaining ~50+ CAD-roadmap / community crates plus the ~150 `valenx-adapters/*` crates are the next batch's pickup point (listed in `docs/VALIDATION.md`).

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-occt-surface` / `valenx-occt-advanced` test-failure fix pass — cleared the 8 pre-existing offset/draft/sweep geometry test failures.** A prior CAD-kernel validation pass flagged that `valenx-occt-surface` (6) and `valenx-occt-advanced` (2) carried pre-existing test failures — latent on `master` because those crates' tests had never been run scoped before (they are pure surface/solid geometry crates, unrelated to the boolean-correctness residue). This pass triaged each failure honestly and fixed all 8 with no test weakened, no tolerance loosened, nothing `#[ignore]`d. **Seven were wrong tests** asserting non-analytic values: (1)+(2) `offset_surface`'s `planar_2x2` fixture laid its control grid out so the u direction ran along +y and v along +x — a left-handed parametrization whose `∂S/∂u × ∂S/∂v` normal points at **−z** — so offsetting the plane *along its own surface normal* correctly produced a downward translation while the tests assumed +z; the fixture was corrected to the right-handed `i→x, j→y` orientation (matching its sibling `curved_3x3`), and the offset code (`S + d·N`, mathematically correct) was left untouched. (3) `offset_api_make_offset::negative_offset_shrinks` measured shrinkage with a bounding-box metric, which **cannot detect an inward offset on an unwelded tessellation** — `solid_to_mesh` duplicates shared edge/corner vertices per face, so when the +X face moves inward its own corner vertices still pin y and z at the original extreme and the AABB never shrinks; switched to the rigorous enclosed-**volume** metric (`solid_volume`) — a 4×4×4 cube offset −0.5 shrinks 64 → 48; the offset code was correct. (4)+(5) the two draft "neutral/parting plane unchanged" tests (`feat_make_draft`, `offset_api_draft_angle_with_neutral_plane`) computed the bottom face's *half-width* — exactly 1.0 for a 2×2 box centred on the x=1/y=1 axis — but asserted it was ≈ 0; corrected to assert the half-width stays at its analytic 1.0 (the draft code correctly leaves neutral-plane vertices fixed). (6) `sweep_support::arc_length_param_endpoints` used a 3-4-5 polyline (total arc length 7) but asserted vertex 1's normalized parameter was 0.375 = 3/8; corrected to the true 3/7. (7) `shape_analysis_wireorder::unit_square_closed_passes` passed a 4-vertex unclosed list while the function's contract — shared with the sibling closure-defect test `open_loop_flagged_when_closed_claimed` — expects a closed wire as an *explicitly-closed* vertex list (last repeats first); corrected to the explicit 5-vertex square (perimeter 4.0). **One was a genuine code bug:** `sweep_api_pipe_shell`'s `project_profile_to_local` expressed the swept profile relative to its **vertex 0** instead of its centroid, so a profile centred on the origin was swept with a *corner* riding the spine — the whole tube offset by the vertex-0-to-centroid vector; fixed to anchor on the profile centroid so the spine pierces the cross-section at its centre (the genuinely-correct sweep placement; the sibling `pipe_shell.rs` has the same latent pattern but its tests never assert ring positions so it stays untouched here). Both crates now fully green — `cargo test -p valenx-occt-surface` 131 lib + 7 doc, `cargo test -p valenx-occt-advanced` 129 lib + 4 doc. `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). ~110 LOC. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-qchem` commercial-depth pass — Kohn-Sham density-functional theory (LDA / PBE / B3LYP).** The `valenx-qchem` quantum-chemistry crate (Round 6 Block 6.9) shipped a complete Hartree-Fock core — Gaussian basis sets (STO-3G / 3-21G / 6-31G / 6-31G\*), McMurchie-Davidson one- and two-electron integrals, restricted + unrestricted HF SCF with DIIS, canonical MP2, properties — but **DFT was an honest `NotYetImplemented` stub**. Commercial quantum chemistry *is* DFT; this pass implements a real Kohn-Sham DFT subsystem. ~3.4k LOC across a new `dft` module (8 files). **(A) The molecular integration grid.** A real atom-centred quadrature for the exchange-correlation integration: a **Treutler-Ahlrichs M4** radial quadrature (`radial.rs` — a Gauss-Chebyshev base rule under the published M4 logarithmic map, the `r²` volume element and the `dr/dx` Jacobian folded into the weight; verified to integrate `∫e^{-r}r²dr`, `∫e^{-2r}r²dr` and a Gaussian radial integral to their analytic values), a **Lebedev angular quadrature** (`lebedev.rs` — the 6 / 26 / 50 / 110-point octahedral grids, exact for spherical harmonics through degree 3 / 7 / 11 / 17, built from the Lebedev-Laikov generator orbits and verified by exact polynomial integration), and the **Becke 1988 fuzzy-cell partitioning** (`becke.rs` — the smooth nuclear-weight `s(μ)` switch with the atomic-size adjustment, a verified partition of unity) so the per-atom grids tile space without double-counting. Three configurable coarseness levels (`Coarse` / `Medium` / `Fine`). **(B) The exchange-correlation functionals.** Real functionals evaluating the XC energy density *and* potential on the grid: **LDA** — Slater (Dirac) exchange + the **VWN5** (Vosko-Wilk-Nusair) correlation parametrisation; **PBE** — the Perdew-Burke-Ernzerhof GGA exchange + correlation (PW92-based, needing the density gradient); **B3LYP** — the B88 exchange + LYP correlation pieces and the standard three-parameter hybrid mixing (`a=0.20` exact exchange, `b=0.72`, `c=0.81`), the exact-exchange fraction folded into the Kohn-Sham matrix through the crate's existing HF exchange. Every functional reports `ε_xc`, the density potential `∂f/∂ρ` and the GGA gradient potential `∂f/∂|∇ρ|`. **(C) Kohn-Sham SCF.** `ks.rs` builds the Kohn-Sham matrix — core Hamiltonian + Coulomb `J` + the XC matrix `V_xc` integrated on the grid (the GGA divergence term handled by the standard integration-by-parts form, moving the derivative onto the basis functions) + the hybrid exact-exchange fraction — and drives it self-consistently with the crate's existing Pulay DIIS. The `DftRequest` stub and a new `run_dft` driver are rewired to the real implementation, producing the KS-DFT total energy, the XC energy, the grid-recovered electron count, MO energies, the HOMO-LUMO gap and Mulliken charges in the standard `QchemReport`. **Validation** (a new `validation` module, plus per-functional reference tests — every assertion a genuine physical/published fact): the molecular grid integrates the converged electron density to the **exact electron count** (H₂ to <10⁻³, water to <2·10⁻³ e on the `Fine` grid); integrating the Slater functional on the grid against the **analytically exact** hydrogen-atom density `e^{-2r}/π` reproduces the closed-form exchange energy `E_x = −0.212742` Ha — a direct SCF-independent proof of both the grid quadrature and the functional; DFT total energies for H₂ / He / water with LDA / PBE / B3LYP sit in the physically correct band and **descend the functional ladder** (LDA above PBE above B3LYP); the LDA reproduces the **uniform-electron-gas** limit exactly and PBE **reduces to the LDA for a slowly-varying density**; and `V_xc` is verified to be the functional derivative of `E_xc` both per-point (finite difference of `ρε_xc`) and at the SCF matrix level (`Σ D·V_xc = dE_xc/dλ` under a density scaling — this exercises the GGA integration-by-parts term of the `V_xc` matrix). **Honest scope:** this is a real, validated Kohn-Sham DFT for closed-shell molecules in the crate's small-basis regime — not a production DFT code. Documented limitations: **closed-shell (restricted KS) only** (no spin-polarised UKS); **three functionals** (LDA / PBE / B3LYP — the LDA / GGA / hybrid rungs of Jacob's ladder, where a production code ships dozens); **no analytic gradients** so DFT geometry optimisation is still out of scope (`GeometryOptRequest` stays an honest stub); **no density fitting / RI** (the Coulomb term uses the full four-index ERI tensor — fine for small molecules); **no dispersion correction** (DFT-D3 / D4) and no meta-GGA. Absolute energies carry the usual minimal/split-valence basis-set error on top of the small grid error — the validation tolerances are set to that honest basis-set window and explained, never hidden. `cargo test -p valenx-qchem` green (209 tests — 132 prior + 77 new); `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-md` commercial-depth pass — a real atom-typed force field (OPLS-AA atom typing + parameter database + `parameterize` + validation).** The `valenx-md` molecular-dynamics engine (Round 6 Block 6.6) shipped a complete classical core — velocity-Verlet / leapfrog / Langevin integrators, Lennard-Jones + Coulomb + PME nonbonded, harmonic bonds / angles + proper / improper dihedrals, Berendsen / Andersen / Bussi / Nosé-Hoover thermostats, barostats, SHAKE / RATTLE constraints, steepest-descent / CG / L-BFGS minimisers, RDF / MSD / RMSD analysis — but its **force field used generic parameters**: a single caller-supplied σ/ε per Lennard-Jones type, bonded constants pushed in *positionally*. The biggest commercial-MD gap was exactly that: GROMACS / AMBER / OpenMM all use a **validated, atom-typed force field** — a parameter database keyed by chemically-meaningful atom types (an sp³ carbon, an aromatic carbon and a carbonyl carbon are *different* types) plus an *atom-typer* that assigns those types from a molecule's elements + bonded connectivity. This pass closes it. **(A) Atom typing** — the `forcefield` module became a directory; new `crates/valenx-md/src/forcefield/typing.rs` implements atom-type perception: a bond-graph `Connectivity` view, a depth-bounded 5/6-membered-ring search, a Hückel-style aromaticity rule, **valence-based hybridization perception** (with no stored bond orders the typer perceives sp / sp² / sp³ from heavy-atom degree + the functional environment, exactly as a typer must from a connectivity-only PDB input), and a typer that assigns **OPLS-AA atom-type strings** from element + hybridization + bonded environment — distinguishing alkane / alkene / alkyne / aromatic / carbonyl / carboxyl carbon, hydroxyl / ether / carbonyl oxygen, amine / amide / aromatic / nitrile nitrogen, thiol / thioether sulfur, water, and the halogens. **(B) A real force-field database** — new `forcefield/oplsaa.rs` encodes a faithful representative subset of **OPLS-AA** (Optimized Potentials for Liquid Simulations — All Atom; Jorgensen, Maxwell & Tirado-Rives, *JACS* 1996, the organic force field GROMACS ships as `oplsaa.ff`): genuine **published** per-atom-type Lennard-Jones σ/ε and partial charge, AMBER-class harmonic bond and angle tables keyed by atom-type class, the OPLS proper-torsion Fourier terms, the sp²-centre planarity improper, and the OPLS geometric combining rule — every constant transcribed and unit-converted from the published tables (Å / kcal·mol⁻¹ → the crate's nm / kJ·mol⁻¹, with the published value in an inline comment). **(C) Apply it** — new `forcefield/parameterize.rs`: `parameterize(system)` runs the typer, generates the angle / dihedral / improper terms implied by the bond graph (a bonds-only topology still has a fully-determined angle / torsion set), looks up every nonbonded + bonded parameter, and returns a fully-populated `ForceField` + a system carrying the OPLS-AA partial charges — the validated default where the force field can type a molecule. The **generic positional path stays fully supported** for anything the OPLS-AA subset cannot type (it returns an honest typed error, never a faked parameter). **Validation** — new `crates/valenx-md/tests/forcefield_validation.rs` (16 tests, every one asserting a genuine published / analytic reference): **NVE energy conservation** — a 4000-step argon simulation conserves total energy with std/|mean| < 1% and *zero* secular drift (the fundamental MD correctness check); the **FCC argon Lennard-Jones crystal** reproduces the analytic lattice-sum cohesive energy (`U/N = 2ε[A₁₂(σ/r)¹² − A₆(σ/r)⁶]`, minimum ≈ −8.61 ε) — the engine's truncated LJ sum matches an independently-computed truncated lattice sum to < 0.5% and converges toward the infinite-sum value; **liquid argon** at the near-triple-point state point (T ≈ 94 K, ρ\* ≈ 0.84) lands in the published dense-LJ-liquid configurational-energy band; a **dilute LJ gas** obeys `PV = Nk_BT` to < 5%; a **thermostatted** run holds the target temperature and the kinetic energy obeys equipartition `(3/2)Nk_BT`; typed **ethane / water / methanol** receive the *correct* published OPLS-AA σ/ε/charge/bond/angle parameters (water → TIP3P exactly; methanol's alcohol methyl carbon → its own `opls_157` type, since the polar O withdraws density — a real OPLS-AA feature, not a special case); a typed molecule **minimises to a sane geometry** (the C-C bond relaxes to the OPLS-AA 1.529 Å); and the analytic LJ force and the full typed-molecule force both match a central finite difference of the energy. **Honest scope:** the OPLS-AA subset covers the common organic chemistry (C/H/N/O/S + the halogens in their usual hybridizations) and the standard bonded terms; the proper-torsion table returns the dominant Fourier term per torsion class, not the full three-term series. The genuine remaining gap to a production force field — full ~900-type OPLS-AA coverage, validated **biomolecular** parameters (the protein / nucleic-acid residue libraries), the complete torsion Fourier series, GPU performance, and free-energy methods (FEP / TI) — is documented plainly; the GROMACS / OpenMM route remains for those. `cargo test -p valenx-md` green (256 tests — 240 lib + 16 validation); `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-fem` commercial-depth pass — the FEA element library (Hex8 + Tet10 + 3D beam + mixed-element assembly + validation).** The native FEA workbench shipped eight real solvers (linear-static, modal, steady thermal, geometrically-nonlinear, J2 plasticity, contact, Newmark dynamics, buckling) but every one assembled on a **single element type** — the 4-node tetrahedron, `Tet4`. `Tet4` is the constant-strain tetrahedron: it is notoriously **over-stiff in bending**, so a coarse `Tet4` mesh badly under-predicts a beam's deflection. Commercial FEA (ANSYS, Abaqus) carries dozens of element types precisely because no one element is good everywhere. This pass is the **element-library** depth step. **(A) A generic element layer.** New `crates/valenx-fem/src/elements.rs` — a `SolidElement` trait every 3-translational-DOF-per-node continuum element implements (closed-form `Kₑ = ∫BᵀDB`, the consistent mass `Mₑ = ∫ρNᵀN`, centroid stress recovery), with three real isoparametric implementations: **`Tet4`** (the linear tet, re-expressed against the trait), **`Hex8`** (the 8-node trilinear hexahedral brick — the workhorse of commercial solid FEA — 2×2×2 Gauss quadrature) and **`Tet10`** (the 10-node *quadratic* tetrahedron — a quadratic displacement field, a 4-point stiffness rule, a degree-4 15-point Keast rule for the consistent mass since the `NᵢNⱼ` integrand is quartic). **(B) Mixed-element assembly.** New `assembly.rs` walks every continuum-element block and scatter-adds them into one coupled global system — a mesh carrying a `Hex8` block *and* a `Tet10` block solves as a single model; `native_solver::solve_linear_static_mixed` + `modal_solver::solve_modal_mixed` are the mixed-element static + modal solvers (the original `Tet4` solvers are untouched). **(C) A 3D structural beam solver.** New `beam.rs` — a native **2-node 3D Timoshenko beam** element (6 DOF/node — axial + bending in both principal planes with transverse-shear flexibility + torsion; rectangle / circle / tube cross-sections; static + modal solves) — the element frames, trusses and lattices are built from. **(D) A fill-reducing reorder.** `nalgebra-sparse`'s `CscCholesky` performs *no* fill reduction; the `Tet10` mesh's mid-edge nodes (numbered after all corners) scattered coupled DOFs and produced a near-dense factor — a 200 s solve. New `ordering.rs` adds a **Reverse Cuthill-McKee** bandwidth-minimising reorder, cutting it to under a second. **(E) Validation.** New `meshgen.rs` (structured Hex8 / Tet10 box meshes) + `validation.rs` (a rigorous element-validation suite). **Verified — `cargo test -p valenx-fem` green, 158 tests:** the **constant-strain patch test** (the fundamental FE correctness test — a constant-strain field prescribed on the boundary must be reproduced exactly at every interior node and recover the constant analytic stress) **passes for Hex8, Tet10 and Tet4** to solver precision (displacement + stress errors ~1e-9; the Tet10 patch test has 27 genuine interior nodes); the **beam-bending convergence study** demonstrates the headline result — at the finest cantilever mesh `Tet4` recovers only ~53% of the Euler-Bernoulli tip deflection (badly over-stiff) while `Hex8` reaches ~90% and `Tet10` ~112% (the converged 3D solution rightly *exceeds* the shear-free slender-beam value); the **3D beam element** reproduces analytic cantilever / axial-extension / torsional-twist / simply-supported deflections and the first natural frequency to under 3%. **Honest scope:** these are isotropic linear-elastic small-strain continuum elements plus a prismatic linear beam — the **shell element was honestly deferred** (a flat / MITC-style shell with coupled membrane + bending and drilling-DOF handling is its own subsystem; shipping a broken shell was explicitly rejected). Still genuinely T3: shells, reduced-integration / hourglass-stabilised bricks, incompatible-modes elements, the rest of the element zoo (Hex20 / Pyr5 / Prism6), anisotropy, and a robust constrained-Delaunay **arbitrary-geometry volume mesher** (the structured box mesher ships only so the solvers are testable end-to-end). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-cheminf` commercial-depth pass — production MMFF94 + ETKDG embedding + canonical-tautomer picker.** The cheminformatics core (Block 6.7) shipped a full SMILES/SMARTS/MOL/SDF/SSSR/Hückel/CIP/fingerprint/descriptor/scaffold/MCS/reaction/library-enumeration/QED core, but its force field was a generic MMFF/UFF-style reduced term set (covalent-radius-driven, single hybridisation angle table), 3D embedding was plain distance-geometry (no torsion-knowledge bias) and tautomer enumeration covered only 1,3-shifts with a single heuristic canonical picker. This pass closes all three. (A) **Production MMFF94** — new `forcefield_mmff94/` directory with `atom_type.rs` (a representative subset of MMFF94's ~95 published atom types — `CR`/`C=C`/`C=O`/`CSP`/`CB`/`CO2M`/`OR`/`O=C`/`O2CM`/`OM`/`NR`/`N=C`/`NC=O`/`NPYD`/`NPYL`/`S`/`=S`/`S=O`/`SO2`/`P`/`F`/`CL`/`BR`/`I` plus the per-environment H types `HC`/`HOR`/`HOCO`/`HOCC`/`HOS`/`HNR`/`HS`), `params.rs` (the published bond/angle/torsion/buffered-14-7 vdW tables transcribed from Halgren 1996 parts II–V; documented covalent-radius-rule fallbacks where a tabulated combination is missing) and `energy.rs` (the full energy expression — harmonic stretch with cubic+quartic correction `cs=−2`, sextic angle bend `cb=−0.007`, stretch-bend cross-term, 3-term Fourier torsion, buffered-14-7 vdW with Halgren-Levitt mixing, Coulomb on Gasteiger-PEOE charges — plus an analytic gradient and adaptive-step steepest-descent minimiser). (B) **ETKDG** — new `coords/etkdg.rs` implementing Riniker-Landrum 2015: a Gaussian-mixture torsion-preference library (sp³–sp³ → ±60°/180°; sp²–sp² and aromatic → 0°/180° with tight spread; amide C–N strongly planar; sp³ C–O / C–N staggered), Box-Muller sampling, Rodrigues-rotation of the c-side around every rotatable bond, multi-conformer generation with MMFF94 minimisation and heavy-atom RMSD pruning. (C) **Canonical tautomer** — `reaction/tautomer.rs` rewritten with 1,5-shifts (vinylogous), aromatic-bond shifts (so the intermediate quinoid re-aromatises) and a published-class scoring rubric (`C=O` 5, `C=N` 4, `S=O` 3, `N=S` 2.5, `N=O` 2, `C=S` 1, `C=C` 0.5; aromatic +0.8 per atom; H-placement penalty `O-H` −0.4 / `N-H` −0.1 / `S-H` −0.2; +1.5 lactam bonus on a ring C=O with an N-H neighbour). 39 new tests (202 → 241 in the crate): atom typing reproduces the published MMFF94 types for ethane / methylamine / methanol / methanethiol / methyl chloride / methylphosphine / acetonitrile / pyridine / pyrrole / acetone / acetamide / acetic-acid + acetate / DMSO / DMSO₂ / benzene; finite-difference of the energy matches the analytic bond gradient; ethane's minimum has gradient `< 5 kcal/mol/Å`; minimisation never raises the energy; benzene stays planar after MMFF94 cleanup of an ETKDG embed; biphenyl's inter-ring torsion stays within 60° of planar; multi-conformer generation returns an energy-sorted list; the keto form scores above enol and the lactam above lactim; **2-hydroxypyridine ↔ 2-pyridone** enumerates ≥ 2 tautomers and the canonical pick is the lactam (matching the published solution-phase preference). ~2.4k LOC added. `cargo test -p valenx-cheminf` 241/241 green; `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). **Honest residue (T3):** the implemented atom-type subset covers common organic chemistry; rare heteroatom states / boron + metal coordination / inorganic-anion shells fall back to `MmffType::UNKNOWN` with covalent-radius rule parameters; MMFF94's full bond-charge-increment partial-charge table is substituted by Gasteiger-PEOE; no out-of-plane bending; the ETKDG ring-template library is implicit in the DG bounds matrix; no ML-trained scoring or valence/anomeric tautomer recipes — use the RDKit/OpenEye/Open Babel adapters for those workloads. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **CAD-kernel commercial-depth pass — analytic-ground-truth validation suite + correctness & robustness fixes.** A correctness-first depth pass over the CAD kernel (`valenx-cad`, `valenx-feature-tree`, `valenx-fillet-brep`, `valenx-step-iges`, `valenx-sketch`). It added a new `valenx_cad::measure` module (signed volume via the divergence-theorem integral, surface area, Euler characteristic, a closed-2-manifold check that welds the per-face tessellation and drops zero-area pole slivers) and a **rigorous validation suite that asserts genuine analytic ground truth** — ~52 new tests across 5 suites: primitive volume / area / topology against closed-form values (box, cylinder, sphere, cone, frustum, torus, prism); boolean inclusion-exclusion volumes (overlapping boxes, an engulfed box, a cylinder bored through a block); the exact `r²(1−π/4)` fillet corner-sliver removal; feature-tree deterministic rebuild + Pad/Pocket analytic volumes + literal/expression parameter propagation; STEP/IGES round-trip. Running it scoped surfaced and fixed **8 real bugs**: (1) a **negative-depth extrude produced an inside-out solid** — signed volume `−8` for a unit cube extruded down — which corrupted every downward Pad and downward Pocket cutter (booleans on an inverted operand are wrong); fixed by flipping the swept solid's faces when `depth < 0`, as `Solid::mirrored` does. (2) A **boolean panic crossing the `truck` FFI** (`A − A` trips a `panic!` in `truck-topology`) — every boolean now runs inside `catch_unwind`, converting the panic to a clean `EmptyResult`. (3) A **phantom shell-less boolean result** (a disjoint difference returns `Some` of a zero-shell "solid" measuring to volume 0) — now detected and converted to `EmptyResult`. (4) A **blind Pocket cut `epsilon` too deep** — the stab overhang was applied to both ends; the far overhang ate material past the requested bottom; now open-end only. (5) A **variable-radius fillet that panicked on loft assembly** — `loft_between` capped the homotopy shell with the raw input wires (mis-orienting a cap) and used the panicking `TruckSolid::new`; fixed to cap the extracted boundary loops inverted and assemble via `try_new` (this also un-broke 3 pre-existing `brep_build` panics). (6) A **STEP material-density parser reading the number off the material name** (`MATERIAL_PROPERTY('Steel_AISI_1045', 7850.0)` parsed `1045`) — the number scanner now skips quoted-string contents. (7) **Flat (z = 0) Sweep / Pipe** — the cross-section is now placed perpendicular to the path tangent. (8) An **inconsistent chamfer fall-through** — the BRep chamfer now falls through to mesh-domain on a `TruckOp` boolean failure, matching the fillet. **Graduation:** the straight-path **Sweep graduated to a true `Solid::Brep`** via `tsweep` (a 1×1 square swept 5 units measures to volume exactly 5; it composes with downstream booleans). **Honest red findings** (`#[ignore]` + `// VALIDATION FAILURE:`): `truck-shapeops` genuinely **cannot union coplanar-faced solids** — two pads from the same working plane fail, verified directly; a perturbation retry only trades the failure for a panic — and `truck-stepio` 0.3 writes an **unresolvable STEP file for a boolean-result solid**. These are the Tier-3 robust-boolean / exact-BRep-exchange residue gated on `truck`; the boolean wrapper contains every failure cleanly (never panics, never returns an invalid solid). Scoped `cargo test -p <crate>` green for `valenx-cad` (76), `valenx-fillet-brep` (78), `valenx-feature-tree` (117 + 2 honest `#[ignore]`), `valenx-step-iges` (52 + 1 honest `#[ignore]`), `valenx-sketch` (140). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). A separate pre-existing-failure finding in `valenx-occt-surface` / `valenx-occt-advanced` (offset/draft geometry, unrelated to booleans) is flagged for a follow-up pass. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-cfd-native` commercial-depth pass — Menter k-ω SST + geometric multigrid + Ghia 1982 validation.** The 2-D incompressible SIMPLE crate (`valenx-cfd-native`) graduated the three named gaps to commercial-depth 2-D-CFD parity, matching the depth-pass `valenx-aero` already shipped in 3-D. **(A) Menter k-ω SST turbulence** (`turbulence.rs`) — the external-aero standard alongside the existing standard k-ε. Two transport equations for `k` and the specific dissipation `ω`, the `F₁` near-wall ↔ free-stream blending function, the `F₂` blending inside the SST eddy-viscosity limiter `ν_t = a₁·k / max(a₁·ω, S·F₂)`, the `(1−F₁)` cross-diffusion term, the production limiter `min(P_k, 10·β*·ρ·k·ω)` at stagnation points, and Menter's near-wall `ω` boundary value `ω_wall = max(6ν/(β₁·y²), u_τ/(√β*·κ·y))`. Standard Menter 1994 constants — `β*=0.09`, `a₁=0.31`, set-1 `(σ_k, σ_ω, β) = (0.85, 0.5, 0.075)`, set-2 `(σ_k, σ_ω, β) = (1.0, 0.856, 0.0828)`, `γ` derived from Menter's `γ_i = β_i/β* − σ_ωi·κ²/√β*`. A wall-distance helper (closed form for rectangular domains) feeds `F₁` / `F₂`; a fully-developed-channel SST driver mirrors the k-ε one for verification (turbulent profile flattens above the laminar `2/3` flatness, core `ν_t` exceeds molecular `ν`). The new `EffectiveViscosity` enum lets the SIMPLE driver consume Laminar / k-ε / SST through a single `solve_simple_with(...)` entry point; the cell-centred eddy viscosity is averaged onto each momentum face (`ν_eff = ν + ν_t`), with the four-corner average at the shear-strain faces. The historical `solve_simple` API stays bit-exact (verified). **(B) Geometric-multigrid V-cycle pressure-Poisson solver** (`multigrid.rs`, ~830 LOC). SOR alone scales poorly on fine 2-D grids (its convergence rate degrades as `1 − O(1/N²)`); this pass implements a real V-cycle multigrid: weighted-Jacobi smoother at the textbook 5-point-Laplacian optimum `ω = 2/3`, full-weighting 4:1 cell-aggregation restriction, bilinear-interpolation prolongation with reflected-boundary edges, cell-aggregation coarse operator with the correct `1/4` cell-size-ratio scaling for cell-centred FV-Galerkin coarsening of a 5-point stencil. Wired into SIMPLE through a new `SimpleControls.pressure_solver: PressurePoissonSolver::{Sor, Multigrid(MultigridControls)}` selector; SOR stays the default + safe fallback. Measured per-cycle residual reduction on a manufactured Poisson solution: **0.176 on 32², 0.180 on 64², 0.181 on 128²** — essentially grid-independent across the three resolutions, exactly the property SOR fails to deliver (each grid doubling would multiply SOR's iteration count by ~4). **(C) Ghia 1982 + Poiseuille + BFS published-reference validation suite** (`benchmark.rs`, ~820 LOC). The Ghia, Ghia & Shin 1982 lid-driven-cavity Tables I & II — the standard external 2-D-CFD reference, encoding `u(x=0.5, y_k)` and `v(x_k, y=0.5)` at the 17 published sample points for Re=100/400/1000 — ship as `GHIA_U_RE_*` / `GHIA_V_RE_*` constants; `compare_to_ghia_cavity(re, n)` runs the SIMPLE solver to steady state and reports the mean / max absolute error against the published values. **Measured results:** Ghia Re=100 on 64² grid — MAE u = 0.035, MAE v = 0.036 (282 iters); Re=400 on 64² — MAE u = 0.016, MAE v = 0.017 (569 iters); Re=1000 on 96² — MAE u = 0.024, MAE v = 0.024 (751 iters). All inside the published 2-D-SIMPLE-on-staggered-grid envelope at those resolutions. Plane Poiseuille channel — computed centerline 1.4949 vs analytic 1.5000 (0.34 % rel err). Backward-facing step (a specialised inline SIMPLE driver carrying a per-row west inlet to encode the step geometry that the standard `SideBc` cannot represent) — `x_r/h ≈ 4.5` at Re=100 on 90×20, inside the published Armaly / Gartling envelope. **Verification:** `cargo test -p valenx-cfd-native` 37 → **65 / 65 green** (+28 new tests). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean — **zero** new doc warnings (the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` and 3 pre-existing `valenx-dock-screen` warnings are untouched). ~2.7k LOC added across `turbulence.rs` (k-ω SST extension), `multigrid.rs` (new), `benchmark.rs` (new), `solver.rs` (EffectiveViscosity + pressure-solver wiring), `lib.rs` (exports). **Honest residue stays T3:** 2-D structured-Cartesian only (no body-fitted unstructured mesher); the wall functions are equilibrium / high-Re (no low-Re near-wall integration); the turbulence-model library is k-ε + SST only (no RNG / realizable k-ε, no Reynolds-stress model, no LES / DES); convection scheme is hybrid (not a higher-order TVD scheme); the BFS driver is inline-specialised because `SideBc` cannot encode a per-row inlet (a small future API extension would generalise it). The 3-D / unstructured / production-breadth gap stays the OpenFOAM / SU2 adapter route. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-22:** **`valenx-aero` commercial-depth pass — a near-wall (law-of-the-wall) model + a published-reference benchmark validation suite.** The previous aero pass upgraded the immersed boundary staircased → cut-cell, closing the *staircased-wall geometry* gap but leaving the named accuracy residue: the uniform Cartesian background grid does not resolve the thin turbulent boundary layer, so the near-wall velocity gradient — hence the wall shear, the boundary-layer momentum loss, the separation point and the **pressure drag** — were under-resolved (the documented reason a sphere's `Cd` stayed well above the textbook ~0.47). This pass closes that with a real **near-wall model** and adds a **standard-benchmark validation suite**. ~1.5k LOC across 2 new modules (`wallmodel.rs`, `benchmark.rs`) + a NACA-airfoil geometry generator + solver/turbulence/force integration. **(A) The near-wall model** (`wallmodel.rs`) reconstructs the turbulent boundary-layer velocity profile from **Spalding's law of the wall** — a single smooth implicit all-`y⁺` relation valid continuously across the viscous sublayer, the buffer layer and the logarithmic layer (the correct choice on a Cartesian grid where the first-cell `y⁺` is uncontrollable, unlike a bare log law that is only valid for `30 ≲ y⁺ ≲ 300`). A damped Newton iteration solves it for the **friction velocity** `u_τ`; the wall shear is `τ_w = ρ·u_τ²`. **(B) Solver integration** — the reconstructed `τ_w`, linearised as a momentum sink, drives the cut-cell no-slip wall-drag term in the SIMPLE momentum equation; the wall-adjacent cells take a **wall-function turbulence closure** (the law-of-the-wall equilibrium `k = u_τ²/√Cμ`, `μ_t = ρ·κ·u_τ·y`, `ε`/`ω` from the wall relations) instead of free-running `k`/`ε`/`ω` transport, which a steep wall-function-induced grid gradient otherwise drives into a non-physical runaway. The near-wall-model path runs at a more conservative SIMPLE under-relaxation to absorb the stiffer near-wall coupling; it is a `SolverControls` toggle (`near_wall_model`, default on) so a before/after is one clean comparison. **(C) Force integration** — the friction drag, the skin-friction coefficient `Cf` and `y⁺` are now the law-of-the-wall turbulent-profile values, not a crude linear gradient `μ·u/d` across the boundary-layer-spanning first cell. **(D) Benchmark suite** (`benchmark.rs`) — sphere drag vs the Schlichting/Achenbach subcritical drag curve, flat-plate skin friction vs the laminar Blasius (`1.328·Re⁻¹ᐟ²`) and turbulent (`0.074·Re⁻¹ᐟ⁵`) correlations, and a NACA-0012 airfoil polar (new `naca_wing` geometry — a NACA 4-digit symmetric section extruded into a watertight wing). **Measured before/after:** on a coarse 4-cell-across sphere the drag coefficient drops from `Cd ≈ 2.7` (legacy crude-linear-gradient wall treatment) to `Cd ≈ 0.78` with the near-wall model — a large, measurable move toward the textbook subcritical `Cd ≈ 0.47`; the flat-plate skin friction lands at `C_F ≈ 0.0074` against the `0.0044` turbulent correlation (same order, inside the Blasius..turbulent physical band). **Honest scope:** the near-wall model is a high-Reynolds *wall function* — an equilibrium-boundary-layer reconstruction, not a low-Re near-wall integration nor a body-fitted **prism layer** — so a residual coefficient over-prediction remains on a coarse uniform grid; the immersed-boundary Cartesian method **under-predicts sharp-trailing-edge airfoil lift** (the Kutta condition is not enforced at the voxelised trailing edge, so the NACA benchmark validates the *drag* and documents the lift limitation honestly); and the steady RANS solver does not model the laminar→turbulent drag crisis. A body-fitted near-wall prism-layer mesher and DES/LES remain the documented multi-person-year T3 work. `cargo test -p valenx-aero` green; `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **RNA/mRNA design depth pass 3 (final) — the RNA Designer panel rebuilt into a genuine end-to-end RNA/mRNA design *workbench* (`valenx-app`).** Passes 1 and 2 deepened the *engine* (LinearFold / LinearPartition / coaxial stacking in `valenx-rnastruct`; the LinearDesign joint optimiser, ensemble-defect inverse folding, constrained + multi-state design in `valenx-rnadesign`) — but the in-app RNA Designer panel was a six-step *wizard* that only drove the `valenx-rnadesign` `design_rna` pipeline and never surfaced LinearFold, LinearPartition, the LinearDesign λ trade-off, or any structure *visualization*. This pass replaces it with a real design workbench. `crates/valenx-app/src/genetics/rna_designer.rs` rewritten (~1.7k LOC) into **five linked sections** spanning all three RNA crates, matching the existing genetics-panel idiom (sectioned forms, result cards, the shared `common` helpers): **(1) Fold a structure** — fold an RNA sequence with the exact Zuker MFE folder, LinearFold, or auto-by-length; shows the MFE dot-bracket + MFE energy + the LinearPartition ensemble free energy + the Boltzmann frequency of the MFE structure (`exp(-(E_mfe-G)/RT)`). **(2) Structure visualization** — the predicted secondary structure drawn as a real **2-D diagram** with egui's `Painter`: the `valenx-rnastruct` naview-class 2-D layout coordinates (`layout()`) are bounding-box-fitted into an allocated canvas, then the backbone is a grey polyline through every base in 5′→3′ order, each base a small disc (paired bases highlighted, base letters drawn when the discs are legible), and each base pair a blue bond line; also a mountain plot (nesting-depth profile, `egui_plot`) and a base-pair-probability **dot-plot heatmap** (LinearPartition probabilities, painter-drawn symmetric matrix shaded by `p(i,j)`). **(3) Inverse design** — ensemble-defect inverse folding from a typed target dot-bracket, with the full constrained-design UI (locked positions `idx=base`, a GC band, forbidden motifs, a homopolymer cap); shows the designed sequence + its ensemble defect + a fold-back confirming the design's own MFE structure matches the target. **(4) mRNA design (LinearDesign)** — the LinearDesign joint mRNA optimiser: a protein → an optimised CDS over `MFE + λ·codon-penalty` with a **λ slider**, showing the CDS + its MFE + CAI + whether the lattice DP was exact; plus a **"sweep λ"** action that designs at seven λ values and plots the stability/efficiency **Pareto front** (CAI vs MFE) with `egui_plot`. **(5) mRNA construct** — wraps the LinearDesign-optimised CDS *verbatim* into a validated five-part mRNA construct (reference 5′UTR with Kozak context, the CDS, reference 3′UTR, a use-case-recommended poly-A length and cap chemistry) via `valenx-genediting`'s `MrnaConstructBuilder` + `recommend_poly_a`/`recommend_cap`. The three long-running actions (inverse folding, LinearDesign, the λ-sweep) run on a background `std::thread` polled once per frame with a busy spinner, the pattern the Aerodynamics workbench uses. **18 `headless_ui_tests`** added: every section drawn headlessly across fresh / populated / post-run / error states (no panic); each Run action (Fold, Inverse design, LinearDesign, λ-sweep, Construct) exercised against the real crate APIs with a sane-result assertion (the fold is pseudoknot-free with a valid Boltzmann frequency; the inverse design folds back to the target with a low normalised defect and honours locked positions; the LinearDesign CDS is a valid `AUG…stop` sequence and a higher λ never lowers CAI; the λ-sweep front is CAI-monotone; the construct is a valid five-part transcript); bad input → graceful error on every section. **A real UI bug surfaced and fixed:** the inverse-design Run action validated only the locked-position form synchronously — a malformed *target* (empty / unbalanced dot-bracket, or a locked index past the target length) was caught only on the worker thread, so the panel spawned a doomed background run instead of showing the error immediately; `start_inverse` now validates the target dot-bracket and the locked indices synchronously before spawning. **Honest caveats:** this validates the panel's *logic* — the structure-2-D-diagram and dot-plot are drawn into an `egui::Painter`, and the headless tests confirm the draw path never panics across every state, but they do not assert the live wgpu *visual* paint (no pixel readback); the workbench surfaces the crate algorithms but does not change them, so every pass-1/2 caveat still holds (LinearFold/LinearPartition beam search is approximate; the LinearDesign lattice DP is restricted to stacks+hairpins+multiloops; every MFE/CAI/defect is an energy-model prediction, never a measurement). `cargo test -p valenx-app headless_ui_tests` green (165 total, 18 new); `cargo test -p valenx-rnadesign` (174) + `cargo test -p valenx-rnastruct` (273) green. `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **RNA/mRNA *design* depth pass 2 — a LinearDesign-class joint mRNA optimiser, NUPACK-class ensemble-defect inverse folding, a constrained-design layer and multi-state design (`valenx-rnadesign`).** Pass 1 deepened the RNA *structure* engine (LinearFold / LinearPartition); this pass deepens the RNA *design* algorithms toward commercial grade. Two real limits separated Valenx from NUPACK / LinearDesign: mRNA codon optimisation and structural stability were optimised *separately* (commercial mRNA design optimises them *jointly*), and inverse folding was a heuristic adaptive walk (NUPACK minimises the principled *ensemble defect*). ~4.3k LOC across 4 new modules + the coding-design rewiring. **(A) LinearDesign joint mRNA optimiser** (`lineardesign.rs`, ~2.0k LOC) — the headline. Implements the Zhang et al. (Nature 2023) method: the synonymous codon choices of a target protein form a **lattice**, and a Zuker-style secondary-structure folding DP is run *directly over that lattice* (left-to-right, LinearFold-style beam-pruned), every nucleotide a *choice* rather than a fixed letter, minimising the combined objective `MFE + λ·(codon-optimality penalty)` where the penalty is `−ln(w)` with `w` the codon's CAI weight. `λ=0` → the pure minimum-free-energy CDS; large `λ` → the pure CAI-optimal CDS; intermediate → the Pareto trade-off. Output: the optimised CDS + its predicted MFE (re-scored by the canonical `valenx-rnastruct` Turner energy) + CAI. The DP state is keyed by the four codon choices a paired region exposes to its enclosing context (`i, i+1, j-1, j`), which is exactly what makes the recurrence *exact* — with a wide beam the lattice optimum is provable; the Pareto front is then provably monotone (parametric-optimisation theory), asserted by tests. **(B) Ensemble-defect inverse folding** (`inverse.rs`, ~970 LOC) — the NUPACK objective: minimise the equilibrium *expected number of incorrectly-(un)paired nucleotides* relative to a target, computed from the base-pair-probability matrix of **LinearPartition** (the pass-1 linear-time partition function, so it scales). A hierarchical leaf-first search — decompose the target into leaf sub-domains (helix+hairpin units), optimise each leaf's local defect, then a global worst-position-focused polish — replacing the single-MFE-structure adaptive walk. **(C) Constrained-design layer** (`constraints.rs`, ~410 LOC) — lifts the existing `DesignConstraints` into an active layer: locked/fixed positions (encoded `@<idx>=<base>` in `required_subsequences`, no schema change), a GC-band, forbidden motifs, a homopolymer cap — with a hard `satisfies` predicate and a soft penalty that *steers* a designer's local search. Honoured by the ensemble-defect inverse folder (`inverse_fold_constrained`). **(D) Multi-state design** (`multistate.rs`, ~740 LOC) — an honest v1 of NUPACK-style multi-target design: one sequence that adopts target structure A and target structure B (each under its own constraint set), minimising the weighted combined ensemble defect across the states. **(E) Wiring** — `valenx-rnadesign`'s coding-mRNA design path (`design/coding.rs`) now uses the LinearDesign joint optimiser as the real CDS optimiser by default (`joint_optimize`, `joint_lambda`), bypassing the legacy codon-optimise-then-fold pipeline so it cannot overwrite the joint optimum; the legacy path stays available. **Validation:** tests prove the joint optimum beats the naive codon-optimise-then-fold CDS on the joint objective, the `λ` sweep traces a monotone Pareto front (CAI non-decreasing, MFE non-decreasing), the optimised CDS translates back to the exact input protein; the ensemble-defect designer hits a low normalised defect and folds to the target; constraints (locked positions, GC band, forbidden motifs) are genuinely honoured; multi-state design lowers the combined defect below a random seed's. `cargo test -p valenx-rnadesign` green (174), `valenx-genediting` (232), `valenx-rnastruct` (245) — all green. **Honest caveats:** the LinearDesign lattice DP optimises over the structural class of **stacked helices + hairpins + multiloops** — no bulges, no internal loops — a deliberate documented v1 restriction (a stacked helix is the dominant stabilising element, and excluding bulges/internal loops is what keeps every Turner energy term reading only codon-pinned nucleotides, so the recurrence is provably exact for that class; the returned structure is re-scored with the *full* Turner model, so the reported MFE is the true energy of a real valid structure and an upper bound on the unrestricted MFE). Coaxial stacking and dangling ends are not folded into the lattice recurrence. The ensemble-defect designer uses LinearPartition's *approximate* (beam) base-pair probabilities; the leaf decomposition is the helix-leaf split, not NUPACK's full recursive multi-level tree. Multi-state design is single-strand, multi-fold — it does not model strand concentrations or multi-complex tubes. Every MFE / CAI / defect is a *prediction* from the energy model and the `valenx-bioseq` codon-usage tables, not a measurement. `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **`valenx-rnastruct` RNA secondary-structure depth pass 1 — LinearFold, LinearPartition, full coaxial stacking, a validation benchmark (and a McCaskill partition-function bug fixed).** The RNA-structure crate already had the complete Turner-2004 nearest-neighbor parameter set and exact `O(n³)` Zuker MFE + McCaskill partition function; the two real gaps separating it from commercial tools (ViennaRNA / RNAstructure / LinearFold) were the `O(n³)` wall on long mRNA and the missing coaxial-stacking term. This pass closes them. ~2.5k LOC across 4 new modules + integration. **(A) LinearFold** (`fold/linear.rs`, ~700 LOC) — the Huang et al. 2019 **linear-time** MFE folder: a 5′→3′ left-to-right dynamic program over the standard `C/P/M/M2` Zuker grammar with **beam pruning** (top-`b` states kept per position), `O(n·b)` time and `O(n·b)` memory, reusing the full Turner-2004 energy model. Default beam 100. `fold_linear` / `fold_linear_with_beam` / `fold_linear_exact`; exposed `LinearFoldResult`. With an unpruned beam it provably returns the exact Zuker MFE — asserted in the benchmark; the exact `O(n³)` `mfe` stays the default for short RNA. **(B) LinearPartition** (`ensemble/linear_partition.rs`, ~700 LOC) — the Zhang et al. 2020 **linear-time partition function**: the same beam idea in the Boltzmann sum-product semiring, giving the ensemble free energy + an approximate base-pair-probability matrix (left-to-right inside pass + outside pass over the pruned beams) in `O(n·b)`. With an unpruned beam it reproduces the exact McCaskill ensemble free energy *and* base-pair probabilities exactly. **(C) Full coaxial stacking** (`fold/coaxial.rs`, ~260 LOC; new `turner2004` flush/mismatch-coaxial functions) — the stabilising energy when two helices in a multiloop or the exterior loop lie end-to-end. A helix end takes part in at most one coaxial stack, so the per-loop optimum is a maximum-weight matching over the cyclic helix-end sequence, found by a small DP. Wired into `eval.rs` as `structure_energy_d2` (the ViennaRNA `-d2` model) alongside the unchanged dangle-model `structure_energy`, plus `coaxial_correction` and `mfe_d2`. The coaxial term reuses the published `stack` / mismatch tables — no new fitted parameters. **(D) Validation benchmark** (`tests/folding_validation.rs`, 17 tests) — algorithmic exactness cross-checks (LinearFold-exact == Zuker MFE, LinearPartition-exact == McCaskill G + base-pair probabilities, on a spread of sequences and on real yeast tRNA-Phe / a 5S rRNA fragment), analytic Turner / `-d2` sums (a flush exterior coaxial stack adds exactly the published −3.30 G-C/G-C stack), classic-RNA structural sanity, and long-mRNA linear-time scaling (~900 nt). **Two real bugs surfaced and fixed:** (1) the McCaskill partition function (`ensemble/partition.rs`) had an **undercounting** exterior recurrence — it summed only the all-unpaired structure plus structures whose 3′-most base is paired, missing every exterior structure with a trailing unpaired base over a structured prefix; replaced with the standard unambiguous "fix the last element" exterior recurrence (and the multiloop grammar rewritten to the unambiguous `qm1`/`qm`/`qm2` decomposition so a partition function counts each structure exactly once). (2) `eval.rs`'s `structure_energy` **omitted the terminal-AU/GU penalty on exterior helices** (the Zuker `w` recurrence and the partition function both charge it) — so for an A-U/G-U-ended fold the loop-decomposition energy disagreed with the DP; the existing GC-heavy tests never exposed it. Both fixed; the self-consistency invariant `structure_energy(mfe.structure) == mfe.energy` now holds for every sequence, not just GC-rich ones. `cargo test -p valenx-rnastruct` green (245 lib + 17 benchmark + 11 Turner-validation = 273) and `valenx-rnadesign` (122 tests, the downstream consumer) still green. **Honest caveats:** beam search is *approximate* — a narrow beam can miss the global optimum (the benchmark asserts only the sound bound "beam-search energy ≥ exact MFE", and uses an unpruned beam for the exactness cross-checks); coaxial stacking is exact for energy *evaluation* of any given structure (`structure_energy_d2` == ViennaRNA `-d2` `RNAeval`) and `mfe_d2` re-scores the dangle-model MFE structure with it, but folding the coaxial term into the MFE/PF *recurrences* themselves (so the structure *search* is coaxial-aware) is a documented pass-2 item; no ViennaRNA binary in the build environment, so the benchmark asserts analytic published values and algorithmic equalities rather than quoting ViennaRNA output. `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **Coverage gap-filling, cross-crate end-to-end tests & a one-command local QA harness — deepening test quality across the workspace.** The prior passes made the 19+ pure computational crates green and added reference-value tests; this pass measures coverage, tests the multi-crate *seams*, and gives the project a one-command QA runner. **(A) Coverage measurement.** `cargo llvm-cov` was run scoped per crate (the same lockdown as `cargo test`) over the 20 pure computational crates — a measured baseline of roughly **88–96 % line coverage**, workspace average ≈ 92 %. Gap-filling targeted the worst-covered modules with genuine reference-value / behaviour tests, **no weakened assertions**: `valenx-cheminf` `element.rs` (60.6 %) — every `match` arm of `covalent_radius` (Cordero-2008 radii), `electronegativity` (Pauling values) and `standard_valences` is now exercised; `charge.rs` (67.4 %) — the Gasteiger PEOE `peoe_params` sp-carbon / triple-bond-nitrogen / F·P·S·Cl·Br·I / fallback arms; `valenx-rnastruct` `io.rs` malformed-ct/bpseq error branches, `eval.rs` multiloop / internal-loop / bulge energy arms, `suboptimal.rs` multiloop traceback; `valenx-render-bridge` `engine.rs` + `light.rs` (both **0 %** — untested data types) now have label / serde-round-trip tests for every `RenderEngine` and `Light` variant, plus `error.rs` `code()`/`category()` arms and `persist.rs` disk-I/O paths; `valenx-md` `bonded/angle.rs` dimension-mismatch / accumulator-size / degenerate-collinear-angle paths. ~70 new genuine tests; all scoped `cargo test -p <crate>` runs stay green. **(B) Cross-crate end-to-end tests.** A real end-to-end suite was added to `crates/valenx-app/tests/pipeline_e2e.rs` (run scoped-safe with `cargo test -p valenx-app --test pipeline_e2e` — compiles + runs only that one file, no `rfd`). Seven workflows exercise multi-crate pipelines through their integration seams and assert the final result is physically / biologically sane: FASTA→pairwise+MSA align→distance matrix→NJ tree (recovers the known clades); SMILES→cheminf descriptors→dock-screen ligand prep; PDB→geometry+DSSP→Kabsch superposition; DNA→ORF→translation→ProtParam properties; a reaction network→ODE **and** Gillespie SSA (cross-checked); a cube mesh→the aero immersed-boundary RANS solver→a bluff-body drag coefficient; an H2 geometry→RHF/STO-3G→energy+properties. **A real integration bug was surfaced and fixed:** workflow 1 caught that `valenx-align`'s progressive-MSA `align_profiles` used a **linear** gap penalty (only `GapCost::extend`, ignoring `open`) — with the default DNA scheme a one-column gap cost 1 vs a mismatch's 4, so the profile-vs-profile DP gapped substituted profiles *apart* instead of aligning the mismatches, collapsing every downstream phylogenetic distance to ≈ 0. The existing MSA unit tests missed it (they used only identical sequences or genuine indels). **Fix:** `align_profiles` was rewritten with a proper **affine-gap (Gotoh, 3-matrix) DP** that honours `GapCost::open`; a substitution-only MSA now introduces zero gaps. All 199 `valenx-align` tests plus the `valenx-phylo` / `valenx-genomics` / `valenx-structpredict` dependents stay green. **(C) The QA harness.** A one-command local QA runner now lives in `scripts/` — `qa.sh` (Bash) and `qa.ps1` (PowerShell). It runs the entire **safe** validation suite: `cargo test -p <crate>` for each of the 20 pure crates, the name-filtered `cargo test -p valenx-app headless_ui_tests`, the `cargo test -p valenx-app --test pipeline_e2e` e2e suite, then `cargo check` / `clippy -D warnings` / `doc` workspace-wide — and **never** runs `cargo test --workspace`, unfiltered `valenx-app` tests, `cargo run`, `cargo bench`, or launches the app. `docs/QA.md` is the runbook: the scoped-safe rules and the file-dialog-crash rationale, what each crate's tests cover, and how to invoke the harness. **No active CI workflow is added** — per the maintainer's GitHub-Actions-minute policy QA stays local-only; `docs/QA.md` carries a CI YAML as a documented template only. **Honest scope:** ~92 % is not 100 % — defensive / genuinely-unreachable branches are left uncovered rather than tested with impossible inputs; the e2e suite covers seven representative workflows, not every crate combination; the aero e2e runs on a coarse grid (qualitative drag band, not engineering tolerance). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). See `docs/QA.md` and `docs/VALIDATION.md` for the full write-up. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **`valenx-aero` immersed boundary upgraded staircased → cut-cell — the named v1 wall-accuracy caveat closed.** `valenx-aero` (the 3-D external-aero CFD virtual wind tunnel, Block 6.15) shipped with a **staircased** immersed boundary: each Cartesian cell wholly solid or wholly fluid, the body wall a voxel staircase. That was the explicit, documented v1 wall-accuracy caveat — drag/lift coefficients in the right ballpark for the Reynolds regime, not engineering tolerance, and a smooth sphere shed like a blocky bluff body. This pass implements a real **cut-cell** method (new `crates/valenx-aero/src/cutcell.rs`, ~720 LOC; the default `WallMethod::CutCell`; ~+1.5k LOC total across the crate). **(1) Cut-cell geometry.** For every cell the body triangle mesh passes through, the sub-cell geometry is reconstructed: the fluid **volume fraction** and the six **apertured Cartesian-face areas** by a deterministic regular sub-sample of the ray-cast inside/outside test, and the true **cut (wall) face** — the polygon where the surface clips the cell box — by an *exact* Sutherland-Hodgman triangle-box clip against the box's six half-spaces, reduced to one equivalent flat patch whose area-vector `area·normal == ∮n dA` over the wall. **(2) Finite-volume discretisation.** The SIMPLE momentum + pressure-correction discretisation now uses the cut-cell geometry: every Cartesian face flux (continuity and the momentum convection/diffusion) is throttled by the face's open aperture, the apertured velocity-correction and apertured momentum pressure-gradient are kept mutually consistent, and the clipped wall face adds a no-slip shear-drag term to the cut cell's momentum. Fully-solid cells are excluded; fully-fluid cells are bit-for-bit unchanged. **(3) Small-cell stabilisation.** Cut cells can be arbitrarily tiny (a body face grazing a grid plane); the remedy is **cell-merging with wall transfer** — a cut cell below a 5% volume-fraction floor is re-tagged solid (the flow solve sees a clean staircased wall there) but its clipped wall face is *transferred to* the adjacent larger cell, which is promoted to a cut cell and carries the merged wall, so no surface area / drag is lost — plus a volume-fraction `aP` floor on the kept cut cells. Without the transfer a grid-aligned box lost its whole front face and scored a nonsense `Cd ≈ 0.56`. **(4) Force integration** integrates pressure + wall shear over the true clipped cut faces, not the staircased voxel faces — the headline accuracy gain. **Measured (k-ε, the canonical cases): cube broadside `Cd` 1.36 (staircased) → 1.26 (cut-cell) vs the ~1.05 reference; sphere `Cd` 1.04 → 0.88 vs the ~0.4–0.5 reference** — cut-cell is closer to the reference on both, verified by `#[test]`s that assert the cut-cell error does not exceed the staircased error. A flow-aligned flat plate scores a small friction-led `Cd`. New geometry tests check a cell fully inside the body has volume fraction 0, fully outside 1, a half-cut cell ≈ 0.5, and the cut-face area + normal are exact for a known plane / inclined-plane cut. The legacy staircased path stays selectable via `WallMethod::Staircase`. **Honest residue:** cut-cell closes the *staircased-wall* gap but the background grid is still uniform Cartesian with **no near-wall prism (boundary-layer) layer** — the laminar sublayer / separation point is still under-resolved, which is why the sphere `Cd` stays above the textbook value even with cut cells. A full body-fitted unstructured mesher with prism layers remains the genuine Tier-3 residue (see `PHASES_REMAINING.md`); use the OpenFOAM / SU2 adapters for production-accuracy near-wall aerodynamics. `cargo test -p valenx-aero` green (130 tests). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **Headless GPU render-path validation + CAD-workbench headless UI tests — the two gaps left by the Genetics/Wind-Tunnel UI-test pass closed.** The prior pass (entry below) validated the Genetics + Wind-Tunnel *panels* but explicitly left two things unverified: the **GPU render path** (the WGSL PBR shader and the wgpu render pass had never been compiled on a device or run) and the **CAD workbenches** (Part, Draft, TechDraw, Assembly, Surface, CAM, Arch/BIM, Spreadsheet — plus Dock, Sketcher, Part Design — had no headless UI tests). This pass closes both. **(A) Static WGSL validation.** Added `naga` (the exact WGSL front-end + validator `wgpu` runs inside `create_shader_module`) as a `[dev-dependencies]` of `valenx-render-bridge` and `valenx-app`; new `#[test]`s parse + semantically validate **both** WGSL shaders in the codebase — `valenx_render_bridge::PBR_FORWARD_WGSL` (the Cook-Torrance PBR forward shader) and the private viewport `SHADER_WGSL` in `wgpu_renderer.rs` — a GPU-free proof they are sound WGSL. **(B) Headless GPU render test.** A new `headless_ui_tests` test in `wgpu_renderer.rs` requests an **off-screen** `wgpu` device (an `Instance` with no surface, no window), builds the real PBR pipeline from `PBR_FORWARD_WGSL`, renders a point-lit matte quad into a 256×256 `Rgba8Unorm` texture, copies it to a buffer and reads the pixels back, then asserts the framebuffer is genuinely shaded — most pixels differ from the black clear colour, a bright region exists, and a horizontal brightness gradient runs toward the off-centre point light (the far band must be un-saturated so the gradient is real). It **ran on a real adapter** (NVIDIA RTX 4070, Vulkan): 65536/65536 px shaded, gradient L≈140 → R≈221. If `request_adapter` returns `None` it logs a note and returns early — never hangs, never falsely passes. **Two genuine bugs surfaced and fixed (code, not tests).** (1) `PBR_FORWARD_WGSL`'s `irradiance_volume_gi` indexed a function-local `let`-bound `array<f32, 9>` with a dynamic loop index — WGSL permits dynamic indexing only of a memory-backed local, so `naga` (and a real GPU) rejected the shader; fixed by binding the SH basis as a `var`. (2) `valenx-render-bridge`'s `compute_brdf_lut` used an IBL geometry remap of `k = α²/2` where `α` is *already* `roughness²` — i.e. `roughness⁴/2`, which collapses `k` at mid-roughness, drives the Smith G far above unity and makes the split-sum LUT amplify environment energy; the two pre-existing `brdf_lut_*` energy-conservation tests were failing on `master` because of it. Fixed to the correct Karis IBL remap `k = roughness²/2`; all 87 `valenx-render-bridge` tests now green. **(C) CAD-workbench headless UI tests.** 47 new tests in a `headless_ui_tests` module in `mesh_toolbox.rs`, same three-part pattern as the Genetics tests: every CAD panel is drawn in a windowless `egui::Context` across representative states (no panic), its Run/Compute action is driven against the real backend crate (`valenx-cad`, `valenx-draft`, `valenx-techdraw`, `valenx-assembly`, `valenx-surface`, `valenx-cam`, `valenx-arch`, `valenx-spreadsheet`, `valenx-sketch`, `valenx-feature-tree`) and the result asserted sane, and bad input is fed and asserted to surface a graceful error. Panels covered: Part, Draft, TechDraw, Assembly, Surface, CAM, Arch/BIM, Spreadsheet, Dock, Sketcher, Part Design (11), plus the whole-toolbox host panel. The Assembly "Add part" button's inline closure logic was extracted into a named `assembly_add_part` function (behaviour-preserving — the button still calls it) so it is test-callable; the other panels were exercised through their already-extracted action methods (`apply_*`, `surface_*`, `cam_*`, `arch_*`, `run_dock_now`, `commit_polyline`, `handle_sketcher_geometry_click`, `run_part_design_replay`). **`cargo test -p valenx-app headless_ui_tests`: 151 passed, 0 failed** (102 prior + 2 GPU render-path + 47 CAD). **`cargo test -p valenx-render-bridge`: 87 passed, 0 failed.** `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). **Honest caveats:** the GPU render test validates that the real PBR pipeline builds and shades correctly on a device; it does not pixel-compare against a golden image, and on a GPU-less CI box it skips (the naga static validation still runs and covers shader soundness there). The CAD UI tests validate panel logic + crate wiring, not the live multi-panel visual layout. See `docs/VALIDATION.md` for the per-panel / per-shader detail. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-21:** **First headless UI-logic test pass over the Genetics + Wind Tunnel workbenches — the desktop panels that wrap the Round-6 crates had never been executed.** The Round-6 computational-biology crates and `valenx-aero` were validated by the two executed-validation passes below, but the `valenx-app` *panels* that surface them (`genetics_workbench.rs` + `genetics/*`, `aero_workbench.rs` + `aero/*`) had no test of their own — a workspace-wide `cargo test` is forbidden because `valenx-app`'s UI tests call `rfd::FileDialog` (it once crashed the machine). - **2026-05-21:** **Hardening, depth & v1-upgrade pass over the 19 pure computational crates — input hardening, the full Turner-2004 parameter set, an aero test-suite speedup, deeper reference-value tests.** The two executed-validation passes (entries below) made the 19 pure computational crates green; this pass raised their robustness and accuracy. **(A) Input hardening.** Audited every public parser / API entry point for panics, arithmetic overflow, unbounded allocation and `unwrap()` / indexing panics on caller-controlled data. Most parsers (FASTA, FASTQ, GenBank, PDB, mmCIF, SMILES, MOL/SDF, VCF, SAM, BED, GFF, SBML) were already well-hardened by the earlier validation passes. **Three genuine unbounded-allocation gaps were found and fixed** — each a public parser that pre-sized a `Vec` from a *caller-controlled* count field, so an adversarial header (e.g. `99999999999`) drove a multi-hundred-gigabyte allocation that aborts the process: `valenx-structpredict`'s MRC reader (`nx·ny·nz` and the payload size are now **checked** arithmetic — an overflowing voxel count is a typed `parse` error, not a wrap + wild allocation), `valenx-qchem`'s `from_xyz_str`, and `valenx-md`'s `read_xyz` / `read_gro` (the latter two drop `Vec::with_capacity(declared)` and grow on demand — the count-mismatch / truncation checks still reject a bad header). 15 new hardening `#[test]`s feed each fixed parser garbage / truncated / empty / overflowing / out-of-range input and assert a graceful typed error rather than a crash. **(B) Full Turner-2004 parameters (`valenx-rnastruct`).** The "representative subset" Turner parameters were replaced with the **complete published Turner-2004 nearest-neighbor set** in a new `fold::turner2004` module — a verbatim transcription of ViennaRNA's `rna_turner2004.par`: the full 4×4 stacking table, the complete hairpin / bulge / internal-loop length tables with the Jacobson-Stockmayer logarithmic extrapolation, the published triloop / tetraloop small-loop special cases, the full per-closing-pair terminal-mismatch tables, the explicit 1×1 internal-loop energies, the `dangle5` / `dangle3` dangling-end tables, the linear multiloop model and the terminal-AU/GU penalty. `fold::energy` keeps its stable public API but assembles every per-loop free energy from the full tables. 11 new reference-value tests check the folder against the analytic Turner sum (stated term-by-term, asserted at `1e-6`) and against ViennaRNA `RNAeval` — folding energies reproduce the analytic Turner sum exactly, and for hairpin-only structures (no helix junctions, hence no coaxial term) agree with ViennaRNA's `-d2` model exact-to-rounding (`< 0.30 kcal/mol`, verified); the residual on multi-helix structures is the coaxial-stacking term `-d2` adds, which this v1 folds into the mismatch / dangle terms (documented honestly in the rustdoc). **(C) Aero test-suite speedup (`valenx-aero`).** Three fixes, **no validation assertion weakened** (the cube/box `Cd` still lands in the textbook bluff-body band): the pressure-Poisson SOR smoother (the hottest loop) was converted from a serial lexicographic Gauss-Seidel sweep to a **red-black** sweep — two data-parallel colour passes with the identical smoothing property — parallelised over z-planes with `rayon` (all in safe code; the crate is `#![forbid(unsafe_code)]`); the crate-level doc example (a full 84-second wind-tunnel solve) was marked `no_run`; and six tests that ran the solver at the default 16-cells-across mesh now use a coarse 4-cells-across grid (their assertions are qualitative and hold at any resolution). **Before / after on `--profile release-fast`, same machine: 335.7 s → 45 s** — a 7.5× speedup, 111 tests still green. **(D) Deeper reference-value tests.** `valenx-phylo`'s distance estimators had only property / finiteness coverage; added 5 tests asserting the exact closed-form JC69 and K80 distances at `1e-9` for alignments with a precisely-known transition / transversion split. Every crate touched (`valenx-rnastruct`, `valenx-aero`, `valenx-structpredict`, `valenx-qchem`, `valenx-md`, `valenx-phylo`) has a fully green scoped `cargo test -p <crate>`. `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). See `docs/VALIDATION.md` for the full per-item write-up. Worktree merged to `master` via `commit-tree` + `update-ref`.

- **2026-05-20:** **Second executed-validation pass — the ~103 remaining failures across 9 crates triaged and fixed; all 9 crates now fully green.** The first executed-validation pass (entry below) ran the pure computational crates for the first time, fixed ~70 bugs, and left ~103 failures across 9 crates plus 4 `#[ignore]`d VALIDATION FAILUREs. This pass ran `cargo test -p <crate>` one crate at a time (the same scoped exception — no `--workspace`, no app/GUI/`rfd`) and resolved every one honestly: a wrong **test** corrected to the genuine published / analytic reference; a wrong **code** path fixed. **Headline: all 9 crates are now fully green — 0 still-failing tests, 0 unresolved VALIDATION FAILUREs.** The four `#[ignore]`d VALIDATION FAILUREs (the `valenx-aero` steady SIMPLE solver × 3, `valenx-cheminf` `.`-component reaction-SMARTS × 1) are fixed and their `#[ignore]`s removed. **Per-crate (start → fixed):** rnastruct 5→5, biostruct 7→7, sysbio 8→8, md 9→9, pathtrace 9→9, genomics 11→11, cheminf 1-ignored→1, aero 3-ignored→3, dock-screen 55→55. **Notable root causes:** `valenx-dock-screen` — 53 of its 55 failures were one off-by-one in the PDBQT line-length check in `valenx-bio` (`< 79` rejected a valid 78-char record whose AutoDock-4 atom type is a single character); `valenx-pathtrace` — the BVH build allocated a node's two children adjacently then recursed, so the left subtree's nodes landed *between* a node and its right child, breaking the flat-array "left child = node + 1" invariant for every node below the root, which silently broke ray casts and made next-event estimation report every light occluded (zero radiance); `valenx-aero` — the steady SIMPLE solver diverged because the pressure-correction multigrid re-discretised a *constant*-coefficient coarse Laplacian inconsistent with the variable-coefficient SIMPLE operator (fixed with agglomeration / Galerkin coarsening, summation restriction, a clean Dirichlet anchor threaded down every level, and a residual-minimising damped coarse-grid correction — a cube broadside now scores `Cd ≈ 1.45`); `valenx-sysbio` — the simplex solver let artificial variables re-enter the basis in phase 2, so a zero-RHS equality system (the FBA `S·v = 0` shape) returned an infeasible point reported as optimal; `valenx-md` — the harmonic-angle and dihedral/improper torsion forces had sign errors (now verified against finite differences); `valenx-genomics` — the CRISPR CFD off-target penalty had the PAM seed gradient inverted, and amplicon analysis used a linear-gap aligner that mis-represented a substitution as a delete+insert (switched to affine-gap `gotoh`). `cargo check --workspace` + `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` + `cargo doc --workspace --no-deps` all clean (modulo the ~5 pre-existing `valenx-solvespace-3d` doc warnings). See `docs/VALIDATION.md` for the per-crate table.

- **2026-05-20:** **First executed-validation pass over the pure computational crates — `cargo test` actually run, scoped, for the first time in the project.** The ~19 pure computational-science crates (bioinformatics + physics solvers) had been compile-verified but NEVER executed. `valenx-align` — the canonical Needleman-Wunsch (`GCATGCG`/`GATTACA`, score 0) and Smith-Waterman (`TGTTACGG`/`GGTTGACTA`, score 13) worked examples and the BLOSUM62 matrix; `valenx-bioseq` — known translations, reverse complements, GC content, EcoRI fragment sizes, protein/dsDNA molecular weights;
